if (is_file('img/activate_ra_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/activate_ra_big.png') != '0070ccc6e8c8db1e7d0d4053ad41a3f19479bd2d')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/activate_ra_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/activate_ra_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/activate_ra_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/activate_ra_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('img/activate_ra_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/activate_ra_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/activate_ra_big.png') != '0070ccc6e8c8db1e7d0d4053ad41a3f19479bd2d') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/activate_ra_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/activate_ra_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/activate_ra_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/error_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/error_big.png') != 'f9ed8cb5be14609addfb37af42310d764a2641d3')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/error_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/error_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/error_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/error_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_2();
if (!is_file('img/error_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/error_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/error_big.png') != 'f9ed8cb5be14609addfb37af42310d764a2641d3') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/error_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/error_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/error_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/forgot_password_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/forgot_password_big.png') != '75c61431e547add81305843d0ab986a76deb32ab')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/forgot_password_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/forgot_password_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/forgot_password_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/forgot_password_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_3();
if (!is_file('img/forgot_password_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/forgot_password_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/forgot_password_big.png') != '75c61431e547add81305843d0ab986a76deb32ab') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/forgot_password_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/forgot_password_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/forgot_password_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/invite_ra_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/invite_ra_big.png') != '4294009194933af279dc5ee71bb9bbe2e9467302')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/invite_ra_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/invite_ra_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/invite_ra_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/invite_ra_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_4();
if (!is_file('img/invite_ra_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/invite_ra_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/invite_ra_big.png') != '4294009194933af279dc5ee71bb9bbe2e9467302') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/invite_ra_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/invite_ra_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/invite_ra_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/object_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/object_big.png') != '4e3e0641152065df4f7895a483e7a8f6ba8cf727')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/object_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/object_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/object_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/object_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_5();
if (!is_file('img/object_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/object_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/object_big.png') != '4e3e0641152065df4f7895a483e7a8f6ba8cf727') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/object_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/object_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/object_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/rainfo_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/rainfo_big.png') != '8acb55c99a1c44aa61b82575f862e9dbcdf3c84a')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/rainfo_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/rainfo_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/rainfo_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/rainfo_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_6();
if (!is_file('img/rainfo_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/rainfo_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/rainfo_big.png') != '8acb55c99a1c44aa61b82575f862e9dbcdf3c84a') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/rainfo_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/rainfo_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/rainfo_big.png');
}

if (is_file('img/register_big.png') && (sha1_file('img/register_big.png') != '368812926fdcff3f4a487fcf117fc1f167a2af10')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/register_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/register_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/register_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/register_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_7();
if (!is_file('img/register_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/register_big.png');
} else if (sha1_file('img/register_big.png') != '368812926fdcff3f4a487fcf117fc1f167a2af10') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/register_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/register_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/register_big.png');
}

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: img/reset_password_big.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('img/reset_password_big.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('img/reset_password_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('img/reset_password_big.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_8();
if (!is_file('img/reset_password_big.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): img/reset_password_big.png');

	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): img/reset_password_big.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('img/reset_password_big.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of img/reset_password_big.png');
}

	if (!is_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png') != 'ec113d8f32e57ddfe903e400170078ed360cd8dd') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png') !== 'ec113d8f32e57ddfe903e400170078ed360cd8dd') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png') !== '6717881d266204202d77a573200f140ed9ac3be2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png') !== 'ec113d8f32e57ddfe903e400170078ed360cd8dd') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/400_oidinfo_export/icon_big.png');
		}
	}
}
